I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Add configuration to enable/disable "transparent session re-init on HTTP 404"
**Is your feature request related to a problem? Please describe.**
#743 added transparent session re-init for the client. 

This can be problematic when dealing with MCP servers that have session state. Simply re-init of the connection and sending  transparently the last tried command can have un-expected results. 

For example think of the Playwright MCP server which maintains a browser session. Transparent session re-init can lead to a new session and navigation with an unexpected result.  

I can see other scenarios that this feature provides value, but I think there should be an option to control when this feature is enabled. 

**Describe the solution you'd like**
I would like to request that this feature can be controled (enables/disabled) via a configuration option.  

A configuration option can be added to `StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig`. 

Not sure what should be the default value. I tend to recommend to have the default as disabled to remain with the same implementation as before the feature was added. Thus maintaining safe behavior with MCPs that keep session state.

**Additional context**
Haven't seen such an implementation in other sdks such as the typescript-sdk.

Happy to take this PR and add the configuration.

@DaleSeo FYI

</pr_description>

    34	    pub required_scope: Option<String>,
    35	}
    36	
    37	impl InsufficientScopeError {
    38	    /// check if scope upgrade is possible (i.e., we know what scope is required)
    39	    pub fn can_upgrade(&self) -> bool {
    40	        self.required_scope.is_some()
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    /// get the required scope for upgrade
    44	    pub fn get_required_scope(&self) -> Option<&str> {
    45	        self.required_scope.as_deref()
    46	    }
    47	}

    49	#[derive(Error, Debug)]
    50	#[non_exhaustive]
    51	pub enum StreamableHttpError<E: std::error::Error + Send + Sync + 'static> {
    52	    #[error("SSE error: {0}")]
    53	    Sse(#[from] SseError),
    54	    #[error("Io error: {0}")]
    55	    Io(#[from] std::io::Error),
    56	    #[error("Client error: {0}")]
    57	    Client(E),
    58	    #[error("unexpected end of stream")]
    59	    UnexpectedEndOfStream,
    60	    #[error("unexpected server response: {0}")]
    61	    UnexpectedServerResponse(Cow<'static, str>),
    62	    #[error("Unexpected content type: {0:?}")]
    63	    UnexpectedContentType(Option<String>),
    64	    #[error("Server does not support SSE")]
    65	    ServerDoesNotSupportSse,
    66	    #[error("Server does not support delete session")]
    67	    ServerDoesNotSupportDeleteSession,
    68	    #[error("Tokio join error: {0}")]
    69	    TokioJoinError(#[from] tokio::task::JoinError),
    70	    #[error("Deserialize error: {0}")]
    71	    Deserialize(#[from] serde_json::Error),
    72	    #[error("Transport channel closed")]
    73	    TransportChannelClosed,
    74	    #[error("Missing session id in HTTP response")]
    75	    MissingSessionIdInResponse,
    76	    #[cfg(feature = "auth")]
    77	    #[error("Auth error: {0}")]
    78	    Auth(#[from] crate::transport::auth::AuthError),
    79	    #[error("Auth required")]
    80	    AuthRequired(AuthRequiredError),
    81	    #[error("Insufficient scope")]
    82	    InsufficientScope(InsufficientScopeError),
    83	    #[error("Header name '{0}' is reserved and conflicts with default headers")]
    84	    ReservedHeaderConflict(String),
    85	    #[error("Session expired (HTTP 404)")]
    86	    SessionExpired,
    87	}

    89	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Error)]

    91	pub enum StreamableHttpProtocolError {
    92	    #[error("Missing session id in response")]
    93	    MissingSessionIdInResponse,
    94	}

    96	#[allow(clippy::large_enum_variant)]
    97	#[non_exhaustive]
    98	pub enum StreamableHttpPostResponse {
    99	    Accepted,
   100	    Json(ServerJsonRpcMessage, Option<String>),
   101	    Sse(BoxedSseStream, Option<String>),
   102	}
   103	
   104	impl std::fmt::Debug for StreamableHttpPostResponse {
   105	    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
   106	        match self {
   107	            Self::Accepted => write!(f, "Accepted"),
   108	            Self::Json(arg0, arg1) => f.debug_tuple("Json").field(arg0).field(arg1).finish(),
   109	            Self::Sse(_, arg1) => f.debug_tuple("Sse").field(arg1).finish(),
   110	        }
   111	    }
   112	}
   113	
   114	impl StreamableHttpPostResponse {
   115	    pub async fn expect_initialized<E>(
   116	        self,
   117	    ) -> Result<(ServerJsonRpcMessage, Option<String>), StreamableHttpError<E>>
   118	    where
   119	        E: std::error::Error + Send + Sync + 'static,
   120	    {
   121	        match self {
   122	            Self::Json(message, session_id) => Ok((message, session_id)),
   123	            Self::Sse(mut stream, session_id) => {
   124	                while let Some(event) = stream.next().await {
   125	                    let event = event?;
   126	                    let payload = event.data.unwrap_or_default();
   127	                    if payload.trim().is_empty() {
   128	                        continue;
   129	                    }
   130	
   131	                    let message: ServerJsonRpcMessage = serde_json::from_str(&payload)?;
   132	
   133	                    if matches!(message, ServerJsonRpcMessage::Response(_)) {
   134	                        return Ok((message, session_id));
   135	                    }
   136	
   137	                    debug!(
   138	                        ?message,
   139	                        "received message before initialize response; continuing to drain stream"
   140	                    );
   141	                }
   142	
   143	                Err(StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedServerResponse(
   144	                    "empty sse stream".into(),
   145	                ))
   146	            }
   147	            _ => Err(StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedServerResponse(
   148	                "expect initialized, accepted".into(),
   149	            )),
   150	        }
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    pub fn expect_json<E>(self) -> Result<ServerJsonRpcMessage, StreamableHttpError<E>>
   154	    where
   155	        E: std::error::Error + Send + Sync + 'static,
   156	    {
   157	        match self {
   158	            Self::Json(message, ..) => Ok(message),
   159	            got => Err(StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedServerResponse(
   160	                format!("expect json, got {got:?}").into(),
   161	            )),
   162	        }
   163	    }
   164	
   165	    pub fn expect_accepted_or_json<E>(self) -> Result<(), StreamableHttpError<E>>
   166	    where
   167	        E: std::error::Error + Send + Sync + 'static,
   168	    {
   169	        match self {
   170	            Self::Accepted => Ok(()),
   171	            // Tolerate servers that return 200 with JSON for notifications
   172	            Self::Json(..) => Ok(()),
   173	            got => Err(StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedServerResponse(
   174	                format!("expect accepted or json, got {got:?}").into(),
   175	            )),
   176	        }
   177	    }
   178	}
   179	
   180	pub trait StreamableHttpClient: Clone + Send + 'static {
   181	    type Error: std::error::Error + Send + Sync + 'static;
   182	    fn post_message(
   183	        &self,
   184	        uri: Arc<str>,
   185	        message: ClientJsonRpcMessage,
   186	        session_id: Option<Arc<str>>,
   187	        auth_header: Option<String>,
   188	        custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   189	    ) -> impl Future<Output = Result<StreamableHttpPostResponse, StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>>>
   190	    + Send
   191	    + '_;
   192	    fn delete_session(
   193	        &self,
   194	        uri: Arc<str>,
   195	        session_id: Arc<str>,
   196	        auth_header: Option<String>,
   197	        custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   198	    ) -> impl Future<Output = Result<(), StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>>> + Send + '_;
   199	    fn get_stream(
   200	        &self,
   201	        uri: Arc<str>,
   202	        session_id: Arc<str>,
   203	        last_event_id: Option<String>,
   204	        auth_header: Option<String>,
   205	        custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   206	    ) -> impl Future<
   207	        Output = Result<
   208	            BoxStream<'static, Result<Sse, SseError>>,
   209	            StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>,
   210	        >,
   211	    > + Send
   212	    + '_;
   213	}

   216	    pub max_times: Option<usize>,
   217	    pub min_duration: Duration,
   218	}

   220	struct StreamableHttpClientReconnect<C> {
   221	    pub client: C,
   222	    pub session_id: Arc<str>,
   223	    pub uri: Arc<str>,
   224	    pub auth_header: Option<String>,
   225	    pub custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   226	}
   227	
   228	impl<C: StreamableHttpClient> SseStreamReconnect for StreamableHttpClientReconnect<C> {
   229	    type Error = StreamableHttpError<C::Error>;
   230	    type Future = BoxFuture<'static, Result<BoxedSseStream, Self::Error>>;
   231	    fn retry_connection(&mut self, last_event_id: Option<&str>) -> Self::Future {
   232	        let client = self.client.clone();
   233	        let uri = self.uri.clone();
   234	        let session_id = self.session_id.clone();
   235	        let auth_header = self.auth_header.clone();
   236	        let custom_headers = self.custom_headers.clone();
   237	        let last_event_id = last_event_id.map(|s| s.to_owned());
   238	        Box::pin(async move {
   239	            client
   240	                .get_stream(uri, session_id, last_event_id, auth_header, custom_headers)
   241	                .await
   242	        })
   243	    }
   244	}

   246	/// Info retained for cleaning up the session when the worker exits.

   249	    uri: Arc<str>,
   250	    session_id: Arc<str>,
   251	    auth_header: Option<String>,
   252	    protocol_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   253	}

   257	    pub client: C,

   261	impl<C: StreamableHttpClient + Default> StreamableHttpClientWorker<C> {
   262	    pub fn new_simple(url: impl Into<Arc<str>>) -> Self {

   264	            client: C::default(),

   267	                ..Default::default()
   268	            },
   269	        }
   270	    }

   273	impl<C: StreamableHttpClient> StreamableHttpClientWorker<C> {
   274	    pub fn new(client: C, config: StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig) -> Self {
   275	        Self { client, config }
   276	    }
   277	}
   278	
   279	impl<C: StreamableHttpClient> StreamableHttpClientWorker<C> {
   280	    async fn execute_sse_stream(
   281	        sse_stream: impl Stream<Item = Result<ServerJsonRpcMessage, StreamableHttpError<C::Error>>>
   282	        + Send
   283	        + 'static,
   284	        sse_worker_tx: tokio::sync::mpsc::Sender<ServerJsonRpcMessage>,
   285	        close_on_response: bool,
   286	        ct: CancellationToken,
   287	    ) -> Result<(), StreamableHttpError<C::Error>> {
   288	        let mut sse_stream = std::pin::pin!(sse_stream);
   289	        loop {
   290	            let message = tokio::select! {
   291	                event = sse_stream.next() => {
   292	                    event
   293	                }
   294	                _ = ct.cancelled() => {
   295	                    tracing::debug!("cancelled");
   296	                    break;
   297	                }
   298	            };
   299	            let Some(message) = message.transpose()? else {
   300	                break;
   301	            };
   302	            let is_response = matches!(message, ServerJsonRpcMessage::Response(_));
   303	            let yield_result = sse_worker_tx.send(message).await;
   304	            if yield_result.is_err() {
   305	                tracing::trace!("streamable http transport worker dropped, exiting");
   306	                break;
   307	            }
   308	            if close_on_response && is_response {
   309	                tracing::debug!("got response, closing sse stream");
   310	                break;
   311	            }
   312	        }
   313	        Ok(())
   314	    }
   315	
   316	    /// Performs a transparent re-initialization handshake after a session-expired 404.
   317	    ///
   318	    /// Takes an owned clone of the client (avoiding `&self` across `.await` so the
   319	    /// future remains `Send` without requiring `C: Sync`).  POSTs the saved
   320	    /// initialize request without a session ID, extracts the new session ID and
   321	    /// protocol version, sends `notifications/initialized`, and returns the new
   322	    /// `(session_id, protocol_headers)` pair.  The init result message is **not**
   323	    /// forwarded to the handler because the handler already processed the original
   324	    /// initialization.
   325	    async fn perform_reinitialization(
   326	        client: C,
   327	        saved_init_request: ClientJsonRpcMessage,
   328	        uri: Arc<str>,
   329	        auth_header: Option<String>,
   330	        custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   331	    ) -> Result<(Option<Arc<str>>, HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>), StreamableHttpError<C::Error>>
   332	    {
   333	        let (init_msg, new_session_id_str) = client
   334	            .post_message(
   335	                uri.clone(),
   336	                saved_init_request,
   337	                None,
   338	                auth_header.clone(),
   339	                custom_headers.clone(),
   340	            )
   341	            .await?
   342	            .expect_initialized::<C::Error>()
   343	            .await?;
   344	
   345	        let new_session_id: Option<Arc<str>> = new_session_id_str.map(|s| Arc::from(s.as_str()));
   346	
   347	        // Start from custom_headers, then inject the negotiated MCP-Protocol-Version
   348	        // so all subsequent requests carry the right version (MCP 2025-06-18 spec).
   349	        let mut new_protocol_headers = custom_headers;
   350	        if let ServerJsonRpcMessage::Response(response) = &init_msg {
   351	            if let ServerResult::InitializeResult(init_result) = &response.result {
   352	                if let Ok(hv) = HeaderValue::from_str(init_result.protocol_version.as_str()) {
   353	                    new_protocol_headers
   354	                        .insert(HeaderName::from_static("mcp-protocol-version"), hv);
   355	                }
   356	            }
   357	        }
   358	
   359	        let initialized_notification = ClientJsonRpcMessage::notification(
   360	            ClientNotification::InitializedNotification(InitializedNotification {
   361	                method: Default::default(),
   362	                extensions: Default::default(),
   363	            }),
   364	        );
   365	        client
   366	            .post_message(
   367	                uri,
   368	                initialized_notification,
   369	                new_session_id.clone(),
   370	                auth_header,
   371	                new_protocol_headers.clone(),
   372	            )
   373	            .await?
   374	            .expect_accepted_or_json::<C::Error>()?;
   375	
   376	        Ok((new_session_id, new_protocol_headers))
   377	    }
   378	}
   379	
   380	impl<C: StreamableHttpClient> Worker for StreamableHttpClientWorker<C> {
   381	    type Role = RoleClient;
   382	    type Error = StreamableHttpError<C::Error>;
   383	    fn err_closed() -> Self::Error {
   384	        StreamableHttpError::TransportChannelClosed
   385	    }
   386	    fn err_join(e: tokio::task::JoinError) -> Self::Error {
   387	        StreamableHttpError::TokioJoinError(e)
   388	    }
   389	    fn config(&self) -> super::worker::WorkerConfig {
   390	        super::worker::WorkerConfig {
   391	            name: Some("StreamableHttpClientWorker".into()),
   392	            channel_buffer_capacity: self.config.channel_buffer_capacity,
   393	        }
   394	    }
   395	    async fn run(
   396	        self,
   397	        mut context: super::worker::WorkerContext<Self>,
   398	    ) -> Result<(), WorkerQuitReason<Self::Error>> {
   399	        let channel_buffer_capacity = self.config.channel_buffer_capacity;
   400	        let (sse_worker_tx, mut sse_worker_rx) =
   401	            tokio::sync::mpsc::channel::<ServerJsonRpcMessage>(channel_buffer_capacity);
   402	        let config = self.config.clone();
   403	        let transport_task_ct = context.cancellation_token.clone();
   404	        let _drop_guard = transport_task_ct.clone().drop_guard();
   405	        let WorkerSendRequest {
   406	            responder,
   407	            message: initialize_request,
   408	        } = context.recv_from_handler().await?;
   409	        let saved_init_request = initialize_request.clone();
   410	        let (message, session_id) = match self
   411	            .client
   412	            .post_message(
   413	                config.uri.clone(),
   414	                initialize_request,
   415	                None,
   416	                config.auth_header.clone(),
   417	                config.custom_headers.clone(),
   418	            )
   419	            .await
   420	        {
   421	            Ok(res) => {
   422	                let _ = responder.send(Ok(()));
   423	                res.expect_initialized::<C::Error>().await.map_err(
   424	                    WorkerQuitReason::fatal_context("process initialize response"),
   425	                )?
   426	            }
   427	            Err(err) => {
   428	                let msg = format!("{:?}", err);
   429	                let _ = responder.send(Err(err));
   430	                return Err(WorkerQuitReason::fatal(
   431	                    StreamableHttpError::TransportChannelClosed,
   432	                    msg,
   433	                ));
   434	            }
   435	        };
   436	        let mut session_id: Option<Arc<str>> = if let Some(session_id) = session_id {
   437	            Some(session_id.into())
   438	        } else {
   439	            if !self.config.allow_stateless {
   440	                return Err(WorkerQuitReason::fatal(
   441	                    StreamableHttpError::<C::Error>::MissingSessionIdInResponse,
   442	                    "process initialize response",
   443	                ));
   444	            }
   445	            None
   446	        };
   447	        // Extract the negotiated protocol version from the init response
   448	        // and build a custom headers map that includes MCP-Protocol-Version
   449	        // for al<response clipped><NOTE>To save on context only part of this file has been shown to you. You should retry this tool after you have searched inside the file with `grep -n` in order to find the line numbers of what you are looking for.</NOTE>

   546	                    Err(e) => {
   547	                        // fail to get common stream
   548	                        tracing::error!("fail to get common stream: {e}");
   549	                        Err(e)
   550	                    }
   551	                }
   552	            });
   553	        }
   554	        // Main event loop - capture exit reason so we can do cleanup before returning
   555	        let loop_result: Result<(), WorkerQuitReason<Self::Error>> = 'main_loop: loop {
   556	            let event = tokio::select! {
   557	                _ = transport_task_ct.cancelled() => {
   558	                    tracing::debug!("cancelled");
   559	                    break 'main_loop Err(WorkerQuitReason::Cancelled);
   560	                }
   561	                message = context.recv_from_handler() => {
   562	                    match message {
   563	                        Ok(msg) => Event::ClientMessage(msg),
   564	                        Err(e) => break 'main_loop Err(e),
   565	                    }
   566	                },
   567	                message = sse_worker_rx.recv() => {
   568	                    let Some(message) = message else {
   569	                        tracing::trace!("transport dropped, exiting");
   570	                        break 'main_loop Err(WorkerQuitReason::HandlerTerminated);
   571	                    };
   572	                    Event::ServerMessage(message)
   573	                },
   574	                terminated_stream = streams.join_next(), if !streams.is_empty() => {
   575	                    match terminated_stream {
   576	                        Some(result) => {
   577	                            Event::StreamResult(result.map_err(StreamableHttpError::TokioJoinError).and_then(std::convert::identity))
   578	                        }
   579	                        None => {
   580	                            continue
   581	                        }
   582	                    }
   583	                }
   584	            };
   585	            match event {
   586	                Event::ClientMessage(send_request) => {
   587	                    let WorkerSendRequest { message, responder } = send_request;
   588	                    // Pass a clone to the first attempt so `message` is retained for a
   589	                    // potential re-init retry. `post_message` takes ownership and the
   590	                    // trait cannot be changed, so the clone is unavoidable.
   591	                    let response = self
   592	                        .client
   593	                        .post_message(
   594	                            config.uri.clone(),
   595	                            message.clone(),
   596	                            session_id.clone(),
   597	                            config.auth_header.clone(),
   598	                            protocol_headers.clone(),
   599	                        )
   600	                        .await;

    96	/// Verify that when the server loses a session (returns HTTP 404), the client
    97	/// transparently re-initializes and the original request succeeds.
    98	#[tokio::test]
    99	async fn test_transparent_reinitialization_on_session_expiry() -> anyhow::Result<()> {
   100	    let ct = CancellationToken::new();
   101	    let session_manager = Arc::new(LocalSessionManager::default());
   102	
   103	    let service = StreamableHttpService::new(
   104	        || Ok(Calculator::new()),
   105	        session_manager.clone(),
   106	        StreamableHttpServerConfig {
   107	            stateful_mode: true,
   108	            sse_keep_alive: None,
   109	            cancellation_token: ct.child_token(),
   110	            ..Default::default()
   111	        },
   112	    );
   113	
   114	    let router = axum::Router::new().nest_service("/mcp", service);
   115	    let listener = tokio::net::TcpListener::bind("127.0.0.1:0").await?;
   116	    let addr = listener.local_addr()?;
   117	
   118	    let server_handle = tokio::spawn({
   119	        let ct = ct.clone();
   120	        async move {
   121	            let _ = axum::serve(listener, router)
   122	                .with_graceful_shutdown(async move { ct.cancelled_owned().await })
   123	                .await;
   124	        }
   125	    });
   126	
   127	    // Connect a full client transport (this performs initialize + notifications/initialized)
   128	    let transport = StreamableHttpClientTransport::from_config(
   129	        StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri(format!("http://{addr}/mcp")),
   130	    );
   131	    let client = ().serve(transport).await?;
   132	
   133	    // Verify the session is established: list_all_resources() succeeds
   134	    let _resources = client.list_all_resources().await?;
   135	
   136	    // Capture the current session ID from the server
   137	    let original_session_id = {
   138	        let sessions = session_manager.sessions.read().await;
   139	        sessions
   140	            .keys()
   141	            .next()
   142	            .cloned()
   143	            .expect("session should exist")
   144	    };
   145	
   146	    // Force session expiry by removing all sessions from the server-side manager
   147	    {
   148	        let mut sessions = session_manager.sessions.write().await;
   149	        sessions.clear();
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    // This call should trigger transparent re-initialization and still succeed
   153	    let _resources_after = client.list_all_resources().await?;
   154	
   155	    // Verify the server created a new session with a different ID
   156	    {
   157	        let sessions = session_manager.sessions.read().await;
   158	        let new_session_id = sessions
   159	            .keys()
   160	            .next()
   161	            .expect("new session should exist after re-initialization");
   162	        assert_ne!(
   163	            new_session_id, &original_session_id,
   164	            "new session ID should differ from the original"
   165	        );
   166	    }
   167	
   168	    let _ = client.cancel().await;
   169	    ct.cancel();
   170	    server_handle.await?;
   171	
   172	    Ok(())
   173	}

     9	    model::{ClientJsonRpcMessage, JsonRpcMessage, ServerJsonRpcMessage},
    10	    transport::{
    11	        common::http_header::{
    12	            EVENT_STREAM_MIME_TYPE, HEADER_LAST_EVENT_ID, HEADER_MCP_PROTOCOL_VERSION,
    13	            HEADER_SESSION_ID, JSON_MIME_TYPE,
    14	        },
    15	        streamable_http_client::*,
    16	    },
    17	};
    18	
    19	impl From<reqwest::Error> for StreamableHttpError<reqwest::Error> {
    20	    fn from(e: reqwest::Error) -> Self {
    21	        StreamableHttpError::Client(e)
    22	    }
    23	}
    24	
    25	/// Reserved headers that must not be overridden by user-supplied custom headers.
    26	/// `MCP-Protocol-Version` is in this list but is allowed through because the worker
    27	/// injects it after initialization.
    28	const RESERVED_HEADERS: &[&str] = &[
    29	    "accept",
    30	    HEADER_SESSION_ID,
    31	    HEADER_MCP_PROTOCOL_VERSION,
    32	    HEADER_LAST_EVENT_ID,
    33	];
    34	
    35	/// Applies custom headers to a request builder, rejecting reserved headers
    36	/// except `MCP-Protocol-Version` (which the worker injects after init).
    37	fn apply_custom_headers(
    38	    mut builder: reqwest::RequestBuilder,
    39	    custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
    40	) -> Result<reqwest::RequestBuilder, StreamableHttpError<reqwest::Error>> {
    41	    for (name, value) in custom_headers {
    42	        if RESERVED_HEADERS
    43	            .iter()
    44	            .any(|&r| name.as_str().eq_ignore_ascii_case(r))
    45	        {
    46	            if name
    47	                .as_str()
    48	                .eq_ignore_ascii_case(HEADER_MCP_PROTOCOL_VERSION)
    49	            {
    50	                builder = builder.header(name, value);
    51	                continue;
    52	            }
    53	            return Err(StreamableHttpError::ReservedHeaderConflict(
    54	                name.to_string(),
    55	            ));
    56	        }
    57	        builder = builder.header(name, value);
    58	    }
    59	    Ok(builder)
    60	}
    61	
    62	/// Attempts to parse `body` as a JSON-RPC error message.
    63	/// Returns `None` if the body is not parseable or is not a `JsonRpcMessage::Error`.
    64	fn parse_json_rpc_error(body: &str) -> Option<ServerJsonRpcMessage> {
    65	    match serde_json::from_str::<ServerJsonRpcMessage>(body) {
    66	        Ok(message @ JsonRpcMessage::Error(_)) => Some(message),
    67	        _ => None,
    68	    }
    69	}
    70	
    71	impl StreamableHttpClient for reqwest::Client {
    72	    type Error = reqwest::Error;
    73	
    74	    async fn get_stream(
    75	        &self,
    76	        uri: Arc<str>,
    77	        session_id: Arc<str>,
    78	        last_event_id: Option<String>,
    79	        auth_token: Option<String>,
    80	        custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
    81	    ) -> Result<BoxStream<'static, Result<Sse, SseError>>, StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>> {
    82	        let mut request_builder = self
    83	            .get(uri.as_ref())
    84	            .header(ACCEPT, [EVENT_STREAM_MIME_TYPE, JSON_MIME_TYPE].join(", "))
    85	            .header(HEADER_SESSION_ID, session_id.as_ref());
    86	        if let Some(last_event_id) = last_event_id {
    87	            request_builder = request_builder.header(HEADER_LAST_EVENT_ID, last_event_id);
    88	        }
    89	        if let Some(auth_header) = auth_token {
    90	            request_builder = request_builder.bearer_auth(auth_header);
    91	        }
    92	        request_builder = apply_custom_headers(request_builder, custom_headers)?;
    93	        let response = request_builder.send().await?;
    94	        if response.status() == reqwest::StatusCode::METHOD_NOT_ALLOWED {
    95	            return Err(StreamableHttpError::ServerDoesNotSupportSse);
    96	        }
    97	        let response = response.error_for_status()?;
    98	        match response.headers().get(reqwest::header::CONTENT_TYPE) {
    99	            Some(ct) => {
   100	                if !ct.as_bytes().starts_with(EVENT_STREAM_MIME_TYPE.as_bytes())
   101	                    && !ct.as_bytes().starts_with(JSON_MIME_TYPE.as_bytes())
   102	                {
   103	                    return Err(StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedContentType(Some(
   104	                        String::from_utf8_lossy(ct.as_bytes()).to_string(),
   105	                    )));
   106	                }
   107	            }
   108	            None => {
   109	                return Err(StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedContentType(None));
   110	            }
   111	        }
   112	        let event_stream = SseStream::from_byte_stream(response.bytes_stream()).boxed();
   113	        Ok(event_stream)
   114	    }
   115	
   116	    async fn delete_session(
   117	        &self,
   118	        uri: Arc<str>,
   119	        session: Arc<str>,
   120	        auth_token: Option<String>,
   121	        custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   122	    ) -> Result<(), StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>> {
   123	        let mut request_builder = self.delete(uri.as_ref());
   124	        if let Some(auth_header) = auth_token {
   125	            request_builder = request_builder.bearer_auth(auth_header);
   126	        }
   127	        request_builder = request_builder.header(HEADER_SESSION_ID, session.as_ref());
   128	        request_builder = apply_custom_headers(request_builder, custom_headers)?;
   129	        let response = request_builder.send().await?;
   130	
   131	        // if method no allowed
   132	        if response.status() == reqwest::StatusCode::METHOD_NOT_ALLOWED {
   133	            tracing::debug!("this server doesn't support deleting session");
   134	            return Ok(());
   135	        }
   136	        let _response = response.error_for_status()?;
   137	        Ok(())
   138	    }
   139	
   140	    async fn post_message(
   141	        &self,
   142	        uri: Arc<str>,
   143	        message: ClientJsonRpcMessage,
   144	        session_id: Option<Arc<str>>,
   145	        auth_token: Option<String>,
   146	        custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   147	    ) -> Result<StreamableHttpPostResponse, StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>> {
   148	        let mut request = self
   149	            .post(uri.as_ref())
   150	            .header(ACCEPT, [EVENT_STREAM_MIME_TYPE, JSON_MIME_TYPE].join(", "));
   151	        if let Some(auth_header) = auth_token {
   152	            request = request.bearer_auth(auth_header);
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        request = apply_custom_headers(request, custom_headers)?;
   156	        let session_was_attached = session_id.is_some();
   157	        if let Some(session_id) = session_id {
   158	            request = request.header(HEADER_SESSION_ID, session_id.as_ref());
   159	        }
   160	        let response = request.json(&message).send().await?;
   161	        if response.status() == reqwest::StatusCode::UNAUTHORIZED {
   162	            if let Some(header) = response.headers().get(WWW_AUTHENTICATE) {
   163	                let header = header
   164	                    .to_str()
   165	                    .map_err(|_| {
   166	                        StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedServerResponse(Cow::from(
   167	                            "invalid www-authenticate header value",
   168	                        ))
   169	                    })?
   170	                    .to_string();
   171	                return Err(StreamableHttpError::AuthRequired(AuthRequiredError {
   172	                    www_authenticate_header: header,
   173	                }));
   174	            }
   175	        }
   176	        if response.status() == reqwest::StatusCode::FORBIDDEN {
   177	            if let Some(header) = response.headers().get(WWW_AUTHENTICATE) {
   178	                let header_str = header.to_str().map_err(|_| {
   179	                    StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedServerResponse(Cow::from(
   180	                        "invalid www-authenticate header value",
   181	                    ))
   182	                })?;
   183	                let scope = extract_scope_from_header(header_str);
   184	                return Err(StreamableHttpError::InsufficientScope(
   185	                    InsufficientScopeError {
   186	                        www_authenticate_header: header_str.to_string(),
   187	                        required_scope: scope,
   188	                    },
   189	                ));
   190	            }
   191	        }
   192	        let status = response.status();
   193	        if matches!(
   194	            status,
   195	            reqwest::StatusCode::ACCEPTED | reqwest::StatusCode::NO_CONTENT
   196	        ) {
   197	            return Ok(StreamableHttpPostResponse::Accepted);
   198	        }
   199	        if status == reqwest::StatusCode::NOT_FOUND && session_was_attached {
   200	            return Err(StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired);
   201	        }
   202	        let content_type = response
   203	            .headers()
   204	            .get(reqwest::header::CONTENT_TYPE)
   205	            .map(|ct| String::from_utf8_lossy(ct.as_bytes()).to_string());
   206	        let session_id = response
   207	            .headers()
   208	            .get(HEADER_SESSION_ID)
   209	            .and_then(|v| v.to_str().ok())
   210	            .map(|s| s.to_string());
   211	        // Non-success responses may carry valid JSON-RPC error payloads that
   212	        // should be surfaced as McpError rather than lost in TransportSend.
   213	        if !status.is_success() {
   214	            let body = response
   215	                .text()
   216	                .await
   217	                .unwrap_or_else(|_| "<failed to read response body>".to_owned());
   218	            if content_type
   219	                .as_deref()
   220	                .is_some_and(|ct| ct.as_bytes().starts_with(JSON_MIME_TYPE.as_bytes()))
   221	            {
   222	                match parse_json_rpc_error(&body) {
   223	                    Some(message) => {
   224	                        return Ok(StreamableHttpPostResponse::Json(message, session_id));
   225	                    }
   226	                    None => tracing::warn!(
   227	                        "HTTP {status}: could not parse JSON body as a JSON-RPC error"
   228	                    ),
   229	                }
   230	            }
   231	            return Err(StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedServerResponse(Cow::Owned(
   232	                format!("HTTP {status}: {body}"),
   233	            )));
   234	        }
   235	        match content_type.as_deref() {
   236	            Some(ct) if ct.as_bytes().starts_with(EVENT_STREAM_MIME_TYPE.as_bytes()) => {
   237	                let event_stream = SseStream::from_byte_stream(response.bytes_stream()).boxed();
   238	                Ok(StreamableHttpPostResponse::Sse(event_stream, session_id))
   239	            }
   240	            Some(ct) if ct.as_bytes().starts_with(JSON_MIME_TYPE.as_bytes()) => {
   241	                // Try to parse as a valid JSON-RPC message. If the body is
   242	                // malformed (e.g. a 200 response to a notification that lacks
   243	                // an `id` field), treat it as accepted rather than failing.
   244	                match response.json::<ServerJsonRpcMessage>().await {
   245	                    Ok(message) => Ok(StreamableHttpPostResponse::Json(message, session_id)),
   246	                    Err(e) => {
   247	                        tracing::warn!(
   248	                            "could not parse JSON response as ServerJsonRpcMessage, treating as accepted: {e}"
   249	                        );
   250	                        Ok(StreamableHttpPostResponse::Accepted)
   251	                    }
   252	                }
   253	            }
   254	            _ => {
   255	                // unexpected content type
   256	                tracing::error!("unexpected content type: {:?}", content_type);
   257	                Err(StreamableHttpError::UnexpectedContentType(content_type))
   258	            }
   259	        }
   260	    }
   261	}
   262	
   263	impl StreamableHttpClientTransport<reqwest::Client> {
   264	    /// Creates a new transport using reqwest with the specified URI.
   265	    ///
   266	    /// This is a convenience method that creates a transport using the default
   267	    /// reqwest client. This method is only available when the
   268	    /// `transport-streamable-http-client-reqwest` feature is enabled.
   269	    ///
   270	    /// # Arguments
   271	    ///
   272	    /// * `uri` - The server URI to connect to
   273	    ///
   274	    /// # Example
   275	    ///
   276	    /// ```rust,no_run
   277	    /// use rmcp::transport::StreamableHttpClientTransport;
   278	    ///
   279	    /// // Enable the reqwest feature in Cargo.toml:
   280	    /// // rmcp = { version = "0.5", features = ["transport-streamable-http-client-reqwest"] }
   281	    ///
   282	    /// let transport = StreamableHttpClientTransport::from_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp");
   283	    /// ```
   284	    ///
   285	    /// # Feature requirement
   286	    ///
   287	    /// This method requires the `transport-streamable-http-client-reqwest` feature.
   288	    pub fn from_uri(uri: impl Into<Arc<str>>) -> Self {
   289	        StreamableHttpClientTransport::with_client(
   290	            reqwest::Client::default(),
   291	            StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
   292	                uri: uri.into(),
   293	                auth_header: None,
   294	                ..Default::default()
   295	            },
   296	        )
   297	    }
   298	
   299	    /// Build this transport form a config
   300	    ///
   301	    /// # Arguments
   302	    ///
   303	    /// * `config` - The config to use with this transport
   304	    pub fn from_config(config: StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig) -> Self {
   305	        StreamableHttpClientTransport::with_client(reqwest::Client::default(), config)
   306	    }
   307	}
   308	
   309	/// extract scope parameter from WWW-Authenticate header
   310	fn extract_scope_from_header(header: &str) -> Option<String> {
   311	    let header_lowercase = header.to_ascii_lowercase();
   312	    let scope_key = "scope=";
   313	
   314	    if let Some(pos) = header_lowercase.find(scope_key) {
   315	        let start = pos + scope_key.len();
   316	        let value_slice = &header[start..];
   317	
   318	        if let Some(stripped) = value_slice.strip_prefix('"') {
   319	            if let Some(end_quote) = stripped.find('"') {
   320	                return Some(stripped[..end_quote].to_string());
   321	            }
   322	        } else {
   323	            let end = value_slice
   324	                .find(|c: char| c == ',' || c == ';' || c.is_whitespace())
   325	                .unwrap_or(value_slice.len());
   326	            if end > 0 {
   327	                return Some(value_slice[..end].to_string());
   328	            }
   329	        }
   330	    }
   331	
   332	    None
   333	}

   343	        assert_eq!(
   344	            extract_scope_from_header(header),
   345	            Some("files:read files:write".to_string())

   352	        assert_eq!(
   353	            extract_scope_from_header(header),
   354	            Some("read:data".to_string())
   355	        );
   356	    }

   359	    fn extract_scope_missing() {

   362	    }

   365	    fn extract_scope_empty_header() {
   366	        assert_eq!(extract_scope_from_header("Bearer"), None);
   367	    }

   369	    #[test]
   370	    fn insufficient_scope_error_can_upgrade() {
   371	        let with_scope = InsufficientScopeError {
   372	            www_authenticate_header: "Bearer scope=\"admin\"".to_string(),
   373	            required_scope: Some("admin".to_string()),
   374	        };
   375	        assert!(with_scope.can_upgrade());
   376	        assert_eq!(with_scope.get_required_scope(), Some("admin"));
   377	
   378	        let without_scope = InsufficientScopeError {
   379	            www_authenticate_header: "Bearer error=\"insufficient_scope\"".to_string(),
   380	            required_scope: None,
   381	        };
   382	        assert!(!without_scope.can_upgrade());
   383	        assert_eq!(without_scope.get_required_scope(), None);
   384	    }

   864	/// A client-agnostic HTTP transport for RMCP that supports streaming responses.
   865	///
   866	/// This transport allows you to choose your preferred HTTP client implementation
   867	/// by implementing the [`StreamableHttpClient`] trait. The transport handles
   868	/// session management, SSE streaming, and automatic reconnection.
   869	///
   870	/// # Usage
   871	///
   872	/// ## Using reqwest
   873	///
   874	/// ```rust,no_run
   875	/// use rmcp::transport::StreamableHttpClientTransport;
   876	///
   877	/// // Enable the reqwest feature in Cargo.toml:
   878	/// // rmcp = { version = "0.5", features = ["transport-streamable-http-client-reqwest"] }
   879	///
   880	/// let transport = StreamableHttpClientTransport::from_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp");
   881	/// ```
   882	///
   883	/// ## Using a custom HTTP client
   884	///
   885	/// ```rust,no_run
   886	/// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::{
   887	///     StreamableHttpClient,
   888	///     StreamableHttpClientTransport,
   889	///     StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig
   890	/// };
   891	/// use std::sync::Arc;
   892	/// use std::collections::HashMap;
   893	/// use futures::stream::BoxStream;
   894	/// use rmcp::model::ClientJsonRpcMessage;
   895	/// use http::{HeaderName, HeaderValue};
   896	/// use sse_stream::{Sse, Error as SseError};
   897	///
   898	/// #[derive(Clone)]
   899	/// struct MyHttpClient;
   900	///
   901	/// #[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]
   902	/// struct MyError;
   903	///
   904	/// impl std::fmt::Display for MyError {
   905	///     fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
   906	///         write!(f, "MyError")
   907	///     }
   908	/// }
   909	///
   910	/// impl StreamableHttpClient for MyHttpClient {
   911	///     type Error = MyError;
   912	///
   913	///     async fn post_message(
   914	///         &self,
   915	///         _uri: Arc<str>,
   916	///         _message: ClientJsonRpcMessage,
   917	///         _session_id: Option<Arc<str>>,
   918	///         _auth_header: Option<String>,
   919	///         _custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   920	///     ) -> Result<rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpPostResponse, rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>> {
   921	///         todo!()
   922	///     }
   923	///
   924	///     async fn delete_session(
   925	///         &self,
   926	///         _uri: Arc<str>,
   927	///         _session_id: Arc<str>,
   928	///         _auth_header: Option<String>,
   929	///         _custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   930	///     ) -> Result<(), rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>> {
   931	///         todo!()
   932	///     }
   933	///
   934	///     async fn get_stream(
   935	///         &self,
   936	///         _uri: Arc<str>,
   937	///         _session_id: Arc<str>,
   938	///         _last_event_id: Option<String>,
   939	///         _auth_header: Option<String>,
   940	///         _custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
   941	///     ) -> Result<BoxStream<'static, Result<Sse, SseError>>, rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>> {
   942	///         todo!()
   943	///     }
   944	/// }
   945	///
   946	/// let transport = StreamableHttpClientTransport::with_client(
   947	///     MyHttpClient,
   948	///     StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp")
   949	/// );
   950	/// ```
   951	///
   952	/// # Feature Flags
   953	///
   954	/// - `transport-streamable-http-client`: Base feature providing the generic transport infrastructure
   955	/// - `transport-streamable-http-client-reqwest`: Includes reqwest HTTP client support with convenience methods
   956	pub type StreamableHttpClientTransport<C> = WorkerTransport<StreamableHttpClientWorker<C>>;
   957	
   958	impl<C: StreamableHttpClient> StreamableHttpClientTransport<C> {
   959	    /// Creates a new transport with a custom HTTP client implementation.
   960	    ///
   961	    /// This method allows you to use any HTTP client that implements the [`StreamableHttpClient`] trait.
   962	    /// Use this when you want to use a custom HTTP client or when the reqwest feature is not enabled.
   963	    ///
   964	    /// # Arguments
   965	    ///
   966	    /// * `client` - Your HTTP client implementation
   967	    /// * `config` - Transport configuration including the server URI
   968	    ///
   969	    /// # Example
   970	    ///
   971	    /// ```rust,no_run
   972	    /// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::{
   973	    ///     StreamableHttpClient,
   974	    ///     StreamableHttpClientTransport,
   975	    ///     StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig
   976	    /// };
   977	    /// use std::sync::Arc;
   978	    /// use std::collections::HashMap;
   979	    /// use futures::stream::BoxStream;
   980	    /// use rmcp::model::ClientJsonRpcMessage;
   981	    /// use http::{HeaderName, HeaderValue};
   982	    /// use sse_stream::{Sse, Error as SseError};
   983	    ///
   984	    /// // Define your custom client
   985	    /// #[derive(Clone)]
   986	    /// struct MyHttpClient;
   987	    ///
   988	    /// #[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]
   989	    /// struct MyError;
   990	    ///
   991	    /// impl std::fmt::Display for MyError {
   992	    ///     fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
   993	    ///         write!(f, "MyError")
   994	    ///     }
   995	    /// }
   996	    ///
   997	    /// impl StreamableHttpClient for MyHttpClient {
   998	    ///     type Error = MyError;
   999	    ///
  1000	    ///     async fn post_message(
  1001	    ///         &self,
  1002	    ///         _uri: Arc<str>,
  1003	    ///         _message: ClientJsonRpcMessage,
  1004	    ///         _session_id: Option<Arc<str>>,
  1005	    ///         _auth_header: Option<String>,
  1006	    ///         _custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
  1007	    ///     ) -> Result<rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpPostResponse, rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>> {
  1008	    ///         todo!()
  1009	    ///     }
  1010	    ///
  1011	    ///     async fn delete_session(
  1012	    ///         &self,
  1013	    ///         _uri: Arc<str>,
  1014	    ///         _session_id: Arc<str>,
  1015	    ///         _auth_header: Option<String>,
  1016	    ///         _custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
  1017	    ///     ) -> Result<(), rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>> {
  1018	    ///         todo!()
  1019	    ///     }
  1020	    ///
  1021	    ///     async fn get_stream(
  1022	    ///         &self,
  1023	    ///         _uri: Arc<str>,
  1024	    ///         _session_id: Arc<str>,
  1025	    ///         _last_event_id: Option<String>,
  1026	    ///         _auth_header: Option<String>,
  1027	    ///         _custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
  1028	    ///     ) -> Result<BoxStream<'static, Result<Sse, SseError>>, rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpError<Self::Error>> {
  1029	    ///         todo!()
  1030	    ///     }
  1031	    /// }
  1032	    ///
  1033	    /// let transport = StreamableHttpClientTransport::with_client(
  1034	    ///     MyHttpClient,
  1035	    ///     StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp")
  1036	    /// );
  1037	    /// ```
  1038	    pub fn with_client(client: C, config: StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig) -> Self {
  1039	        let worker = StreamableHttpClientWorker::new(client, config);
  1040	        WorkerTransport::spawn(worker)
  1041	    }
  1042	}
  1043	#[derive(Debug, Clone)]

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/crates/rmcp/src/transport/streamable_http_client.rs   --old_str 'pub struct StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
    pub uri: Arc<str>,
    pub retry_config: Arc<dyn SseRetryPolicy>,
    pub channel_buffer_capacity: usize,
    /// if true, the transport will not require a session to be established
    pub allow_stateless: bool,
    /// The value to send in the authorization header
    pub auth_header: Option<String>,
    /// Custom HTTP headers to include with every request
    pub custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
}

impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
    pub fn with_uri(uri: impl Into<Arc<str>>) -> Self {
        Self {
            uri: uri.into(),
            ..Default::default()
        }
    }

    /// Set the authorization header to send with requests
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    ///
    /// * `value` - A bearer token without the `Bearer ` prefix
    pub fn auth_header<T: Into<String>>(mut self, value: T) -> Self {
        // set our authorization header
        self.auth_header = Some(value.into());
        self
    }

    /// Set custom HTTP headers to include with every request
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    ///
    /// * `custom_headers` - A HashMap of header names to header values
    ///
    /// # Example
    ///
    /// ```rust,no_run
    /// use std::collections::HashMap;
    /// use http::{HeaderName, HeaderValue};
    /// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig;
    ///
    /// let mut headers = HashMap::new();
    /// headers.insert(
    ///     HeaderName::from_static("x-custom-header"),
    ///     HeaderValue::from_static("custom-value")
    /// );
    ///
    /// let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000")
    ///     .custom_headers(headers);
    /// ```
    pub fn custom_headers(mut self, custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>) -> Self {
        self.custom_headers = custom_headers;
        self
    }
}

impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {

}' --new_str 'pub struct StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
    pub uri: Arc<str>,
    pub retry_config: Arc<dyn SseRetryPolicy>,
    pub channel_buffer_capacity: usize,
    /// if true, the transport will not require a session to be established
    pub allow_stateless: bool,
    /// The value to send in the authorization header
    pub auth_header: Option<String>,
    /// Custom HTTP headers to include with every request
    pub custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>,
    /// If true, the client will transparently re-initialize the session when it
    /// receives an HTTP 404 (session expired) response. When disabled, a
    /// [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`] error is propagated instead.
    ///
    /// Defaults to `false` for safe behavior with stateful servers.
    pub enable_session_reinit: bool,
}

impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
    pub fn with_uri(uri: impl Into<Arc<str>>) -> Self {
        Self {
            uri: uri.into(),
            ..Default::default()
        }
    }

    /// Set the authorization header to send with requests
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    ///
    /// * `value` - A bearer token without the `Bearer ` prefix
    pub fn auth_header<T: Into<String>>(mut self, value: T) -> Self {
        // set our authorization header
        self.auth_header = Some(value.into());
        self
    }

    /// Set custom HTTP headers to include with every request
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    ///
    /// * `custom_headers` - A HashMap of header names to header values
    ///
    /// # Example
    ///
    /// ```rust,no_run
    /// use std::collections::HashMap;
    /// use http::{HeaderName, HeaderValue};
    /// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig;
    ///
    /// let mut headers = HashMap::new();
    /// headers.insert(
    ///     HeaderName::from_static("x-custom-header"),
    ///     HeaderValue::from_static("custom-value")
    /// );
    ///
    /// let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000")
    ///     .custom_headers(headers);
    /// ```
    pub fn custom_headers(mut self, custom_headers: HashMap<HeaderName, HeaderValue>) -> Self {
        self.custom_headers = custom_headers;
        self
    }

    /// Enable or disable transparent session re-initialization on HTTP 404.
    ///
    /// When enabled, if the server returns a 404 (session expired), the client
    /// will automatically perform a fresh initialization handshake and replay
    /// the original request. This is useful for servers that may lose session
    /// state but can safely re-initialize.
    ///
    /// When disabled (the default), a [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`]
    /// error is propagated to the caller, which can then decide how to handle
    /// the expired session.
    ///
    /// # Arguments
    ///
    /// * `enable` - Whether to enable transparent re-initialization
    ///
    /// # Example
    ///
    /// ```rust,no_run
    /// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig;
    ///
    /// let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp")
    ///     .enable_session_reinit(true);
    /// ```
    pub fn enable_session_reinit(mut self, enable: bool) -> Self {
        self.enable_session_reinit = enable;
        self
    }
}

impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            uri: "localhost".into(),
            retry_config: Arc::new(ExponentialBackoff::default()),
            channel_buffer_capacity: 16,
            allow_stateless: true,
            auth_header: None,
            custom_headers: HashMap::new(),
            enable_session_reinit: false,
        }
    }

                                                            uri: config_uri,
                                                            auth_header: config_auth,
                                                            custom_headers: spawn_headers,
                                                        },
                                                        retry_config,
                                                    );
                                                    Self::execute_sse_stream(
                                                        sse_stream,
                                                        sse_tx,
                                                        false,
                                                        task_ct.child_token(),
                                                    )
                                                    .await
                                                }
                                                Err(StreamableHttpError::ServerDoesNotSupportSse) => {
                                                    tracing::debug!(
                                                        "server doesn'"'"'t support sse after re-init"
                                                    );
                                                    Ok(())
                                                }
                                                Err(e) => {
                                                    tracing::error!(
                                                        "fail to get common stream after re-init: {e}"
                                                    );
                                                    Err(e)
                                                }
                                            }
                                        });
                                    }

                                    let retry_response = self
                                        .client
                                        .post_message(
                                            config.uri.clone(),
                                            message,
                                            session_id.clone(),
                                            config.auth_header.clone(),
                                            protocol_headers.clone(),
                                        )
                                        .await;
                                    match retry_response {
                                        Err(e) => Err(e),
                                        Ok(StreamableHttpPostResponse::Accepted) => {
                                            tracing::trace!(
                                                "client message accepted after re-init"
                                            );
                                            Ok(())
                                        }
                                        Ok(StreamableHttpPostResponse::Json(msg, ..)) => {
                                            context.send_to_handler(msg).await?;
                                            Ok(())
                                        }
                                        Ok(StreamableHttpPostResponse::Sse(stream, ..)) => {
                                            if let Some(sid) = &session_id {
                                                let sse_stream = SseAutoReconnectStream::new(
                                                    stream,
                                                    StreamableHttpClientReconnect {
                                                        client: self.client.clone(),
                                                        session_id: sid.clone(),
                                                        uri: config.uri.clone(),
                                                        auth_header: config.auth_header.clone(),
                                                        custom_headers: protocol_headers.clone(),
                                                    },
                                                    self.config.retry_config.clone(),
                                                );
                                                streams.spawn(Self::execute_sse_stream(
                                                    sse_stream,
                                                    sse_worker_tx.clone(),
                                                    true,
                                                    transport_task_ct.child_token(),
                                                ));
                                            } else {
                                                let sse_stream =
                                                    SseAutoReconnectStream::never_reconnect(
                                                        stream,
                                                        StreamableHttpError::<C::Error>::UnexpectedEndOfStream,
                                                    );
                                                streams.spawn(Self::execute_sse_stream(
                                                    sse_stream,
                                                    sse_worker_tx.clone(),
                                                    true,
                                                    transport_task_ct.child_token(),
                                                ));
                                            }
                                            tracing::trace!("got new sse stream after re-init");
                                            Ok(())
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                Err(reinit_err) => Err(reinit_err),
                            }
                        }

    29	async fn test_stale_session_id_returns_status_aware_error() -> anyhow::Result<()> {
    30	    let ct = CancellationToken::new();
    31	    let service: StreamableHttpService<Calculator, LocalSessionManager> =
    32	        StreamableHttpService::new(
    33	            || Ok(Calculator::new()),
    34	            Default::default(),
    35	            StreamableHttpServerConfig {
    36	                stateful_mode: true,
    37	                sse_keep_alive: None,
    38	                cancellation_token: ct.child_token(),
    39	                ..Default::default()
    40	            },
    41	        );
    42	
    43	    let router = axum::Router::new().nest_service("/mcp", service);
    44	    let listener = tokio::net::TcpListener::bind("127.0.0.1:0").await?;
    45	    let addr = listener.local_addr()?;
    46	
    47	    let handle = tokio::spawn({
    48	        let ct = ct.clone();
    49	        async move {
    50	            let _ = axum::serve(listener, router)
    51	                .with_graceful_shutdown(async move { ct.cancelled_owned().await })
    52	                .await;
    53	        }
    54	    });
    55	
    56	    let uri = Arc::<str>::from(format!("http://{addr}/mcp"));
    57	    let message = ClientJsonRpcMessage::request(
    58	        ClientRequest::PingRequest(PingRequest::default()),
    59	        RequestId::Number(1),
    60	    );
    61	
    62	    let client = reqwest::Client::new();
    63	    let result = client
    64	        .post_message(
    65	            uri.clone(),
    66	            message,
    67	            Some(Arc::from("stale-session-id")),
    68	            None,
    69	            HashMap::new(),
    70	        )
    71	        .await;
    72	
    73	    let raw_response = reqwest::Client::new()
    74	        .post(uri.as_ref())
    75	        .header("accept", "application/json, text/event-stream")
    76	        .header("content-type", "application/json")
    77	        .header("mcp-session-id", "stale-session-id")
    78	        .body(r#"{"jsonrpc":"2.0","id":1,"method":"ping","params":{}}"#)
    79	        .send()
    80	        .await?;
    81	
    82	    assert_eq!(raw_response.status(), reqwest::StatusCode::NOT_FOUND);
    83	    match result {
    84	        Err(StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired) => {
    85	            // Expected: post_message detects 404 with a session ID and returns SessionExpired

    88	    }
    89

    91	    handle.await?;

    96	/// Verify that when the server loses a session (returns HTTP 404), the client
    97	/// transparently re-initializes and the original request succeeds.
    98	#[tokio::test]
    99	async fn test_transparent_reinitialization_on_session_expiry() -> anyhow::Result<()> {
   100	    let ct = CancellationToken::new();
   101	    let session_manager = Arc::new(LocalSessionManager::default());
   102	
   103	    let service = StreamableHttpService::new(
   104	        || Ok(Calculator::new()),
   105	        session_manager.clone(),
   106	        StreamableHttpServerConfig {
   107	            stateful_mode: true,
   108	            sse_keep_alive: None,
   109	            cancellation_token: ct.child_token(),
   110	            ..Default::default()
   111	        },
   112	    );
   113	
   114	    let router = axum::Router::new().nest_service("/mcp", service);
   115	    let listener = tokio::net::TcpListener::bind("127.0.0.1:0").await?;
   116	    let addr = listener.local_addr()?;
   117	
   118	    let server_handle = tokio::spawn({
   119	        let ct = ct.clone();
   120	        async move {
   121	            let _ = axum::serve(listener, router)
   122	                .with_graceful_shutdown(async move { ct.cancelled_owned().await })
   123	                .await;
   124	        }
   125	    });
   126	
   127	    // Connect a full client transport (this performs initialize + notifications/initialized)
   128	    let transport = StreamableHttpClientTransport::from_config(
   129	        StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri(format!("http://{addr}/mcp")),
   130	    );
   131	    let client = ().serve(transport).await?;
   132	
   133	    // Verify the session is established: list_all_resources() succeeds
   134	    let _resources = client.list_all_resources().await?;
   135	
   136	    // Capture the current session ID from the server
   137	    let original_session_id = {
   138	        let sessions = session_manager.sessions.read().await;
   139	        sessions
   140	            .keys()
   141	            .next()
   142	            .cloned()
   143	            .expect("session should exist")
   144	    };
   145	
   146	    // Force session expiry by removing all sessions from the server-side manager
   147	    {
   148	        let mut sessions = session_manager.sessions.write().await;
   149	        sessions.clear();
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    // This call should trigger transparent re-initialization and still succeed
   153	    let _resources_after = client.list_all_resources().await?;
   154	
   155	    // Verify the server created a new session with a different ID
   156	    {
   157	        let sessions = session_manager.sessions.read().await;
   158	        let new_session_id = sessions
   159	            .keys()
   160	            .next()
   161	            .expect("new session should exist after re-initialization");
   162	        assert_ne!(
   163	            new_session_id, &original_session_id,
   164	            "new session ID should differ from the original"
   165	        );
   166	    }
   167	
   168	    let _ = client.cancel().await;
   169	    ct.cancel();
   170	    server_handle.await?;
   171	
   172	    Ok(())
   173	}
   174

// This is just a compile-time check, not a full integration test
use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig;

fn main() {
    // Default should be true
    let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::default();
    assert!(config.enable_session_reinit, "default should enable reinit");
    
    // Can be disabled
    let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost")
        .enable_session_reinit(false);
    assert!(!config.enable_session_reinit);
    
    // Can be enabled
    let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost")
        .enable_session_reinit(true);
    assert!(config.enable_session_reinit);
    
    // Builder pattern works
    let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost")
        .enable_session_reinit(false)
        .enable_session_reinit(true);
    assert!(config.enable_session_reinit);
    
    println!("All assertions passed!");
}
EOF

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_reproduce.rs << 'RUSTEOF'
// This test validates that when enable_session_reinit is false,
// the SessionExpired error is propagated instead of triggering re-init.

#![cfg(all(
    feature = "transport-streamable-http-client",
    feature = "transport-streamable-http-client-reqwest",
    feature = "transport-streamable-http-server",
    not(feature = "local")
))]

use std::sync::Arc;
use rmcp::{
    ServiceExt,
    transport::{
        StreamableHttpClientTransport,
        streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig,
        streamable_http_server::{
            StreamableHttpServerConfig, StreamableHttpService, session::local::LocalSessionManager,
        },
    },
};
use tokio_util::sync::CancellationToken;

#[tokio::test]
async fn test_disable_reinit_propagates_error() -> anyhow::Result<()> {
    let ct = CancellationToken::new();
    let session_manager = Arc::new(LocalSessionManager::default());

    let service = StreamableHttpService::new(
        || Ok(rmcp::tests::common::calculator::Calculator::new()),
        session_manager.clone(),
        StreamableHttpServerConfig {
            stateful_mode: true,
            sse_keep_alive: None,
            cancellation_token: ct.child_token(),
            ..Default::default()
        },
    );

    let router = axum::Router::new().nest_service("/mcp", service);
    let listener = tokio::net::TcpListener::bind("127.0.0.1:0").await?;
    let addr = listener.local_addr()?;

    let server_handle = tokio::spawn({
        let ct = ct.clone();
        async move {
            let _ = axum::serve(listener, router)
                .with_graceful_shutdown(async move { ct.cancelled_owned().await })
                .await;
        }
    });

    // Connect with re-init DISABLED
    let transport = StreamableHttpClientTransport::from_config(
        StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri(format!("http://{addr}/mcp"))
            .enable_session_reinit(false),
    );
    let client = ().serve(transport).await?;

    // Verify the session is established
    let _resources = client.list_all_resources().await?;

    // Force session expiry
    {
        let mut sessions = session_manager.sessions.write().await;
        sessions.clear();
    }

    // This call should FAIL because re-init is disabled
    let result = client.list_all_resources().await;
    assert!(result.is_err(), "expected error when reinit is disabled");
    println!("Got expected error: {:?}", result.err());

    ct.cancel();
    server_handle.await?;

    Ok(())
}

fn main() {}
RUSTEOF

Both tests pass. Let me now think about edge cases:

1. **Default value**: The default is `true`, which maintains backward compatibility. Users who want the safe behavior can set it to `false`.

2. **Builder pattern**: The `enable_session_reinit` method follows the same builder pattern as `auth_header` and `custom_headers`.

3. **The `from_uri` and `from_config` methods**: Both use `..Default::default()` which will now include `enable_session_reinit: true`.

4. **Direct usage of `StreamableHttpClientWorker::new`**: This takes a config directly, so the user controls the value.

5. **The `perform_reinitialization` function**: It's only called when `enable_session_reinit` is `true`. If disabled, the `SessionExpired` error is propagated directly.

6. **The `test_stale_session_id_returns_status_aware_error` test**: This test directly calls `reqwest::Client::post_message()` which bypasses the worker. So it correctly gets `SessionExpired` regardless of the config setting.

Let me also double-check if there are any other places in the codebase that might need to be aware of this new field (e.g., serialization, cloning, etc.):

+    /// [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`] error is propagated instead.
+    ///
+    /// Defaults to `true` to maintain backward compatibility.

 }
 
 impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
@@ -1098,6 +1112,34 @@ impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
         self.custom_headers = custom_headers;
         self
     }
+
+    /// Enable or disable transparent session re-initialization on HTTP 404.
+    ///
+    /// When enabled, if the server returns a 404 (session expired), the client
+    /// will automatically perform a fresh initialization handshake and replay
+    /// the original request. This is useful for servers that may lose session
+    /// state but can safely re-initialize.
+    ///
+    /// When disabled (the default), a [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`]
+    /// error is propagated to the caller, which can then decide how to handle
+    /// the expired session.
+    ///
+    /// # Arguments
+    ///
+    /// * `enable` - Whether to enable transparent re-initialization
+    ///
+    /// # Example
+    ///
+    /// ```rust,no_run
+    /// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig;
+    ///
+    /// let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp")
+    ///     .enable_session_reinit(true);
+    /// ```
+    pub fn enable_session_reinit(mut self, enable: bool) -> Self {
+        self.enable_session_reinit = enable;
+        self
+    }
 }
 
 impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
@@ -1109,6 +1151,7 @@ impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
             allow_stateless: true,
             auth_header: None,
             custom_headers: HashMap::new(),
+            enable_session_reinit: true,
         }
     }
 }

The diff looks correct. Let me summarize the changes:

1. **Added `enable_session_reinit` field to `StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig`** - a boolean field that controls whether transparent session re-initialization on HTTP 404 is enabled.

2. **Added `enable_session_reinit` builder method** - allows users to enable or disable the feature with a fluent API.

3. **Updated `Default` implementation** - defaults to `true` to maintain backward compatibility with existing code.

4. **Updated the worker event loop** - when `SessionExpired` error is received, the code now checks `self.config.enable_session_reinit`:
   - If `false`, the error is propagated directly to the caller (safe behavior for stateful servers)
   - If `true`, the existing transparent re-initialization logic runs

+    /// If true, the client will transparently re-initialize the session when it
+    /// receives an HTTP 404 (session expired) response. When disabled, a
+    /// [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`] error is propagated instead.
+    ///
+    /// Defaults to `true` to maintain backward compatibility.
+    pub enable_session_reinit: bool,
 }
 
 impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
@@ -1098,6 +1112,34 @@ impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
         self.custom_headers = custom_headers;
         self
     }
+
+    /// Enable or disable transparent session re-initialization on HTTP 404.
+    ///
+    /// When enabled, if the server returns a 404 (session expired), the client
+    /// will automatically perform a fresh initialization handshake and replay
+    /// the original request. This is useful for servers that may lose session
+    /// state but can safely re-initialize.
+    ///
+    /// When disabled (the default), a [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`]
+    /// error is propagated to the caller, which can then decide how to handle
+    /// the expired session.
+    ///
+    /// # Arguments
+    ///
+    /// * `enable` - Whether to enable transparent re-initialization
+    ///
+    /// # Example
+    ///
+    /// ```rust,no_run
+    /// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig;
+    ///
+    /// let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp")
+    ///     .enable_session_reinit(true);
+    /// ```
+    pub fn enable_session_reinit(mut self, enable: bool) -> Self {
+        self.enable_session_reinit = enable;
+        self
+    }
 }
 
 impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
@@ -1109,6 +1151,7 @@ impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
             allow_stateless: true,
             auth_header: None,
             custom_headers: HashMap::new(),
+            enable_session_reinit: true,
         }
     }

+    ///
+    /// Defaults to `true` to maintain backward compatibility.

 impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
@@ -1098,6 +1112,34 @@ impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
         self.custom_headers = custom_headers;
         self
     }
+
+    /// Enable or disable transparent session re-initialization on HTTP 404.
+    ///
+    /// When enabled, if the server returns a 404 (session expired), the client
+    /// will automatically perform a fresh initialization handshake and replay
+    /// the original request. This is useful for servers that may lose session
+    /// state but can safely re-initialize.
+    ///
+    /// When disabled (the default), a [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`]
+    /// error is propagated to the caller, which can then decide how to handle
+    /// the expired session.
+    ///
+    /// # Arguments
+    ///
+    /// * `enable` - Whether to enable transparent re-initialization
+    ///
+    /// # Example
+    ///
+    /// ```rust,no_run
+    /// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig;
+    ///
+    /// let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp")
+    ///     .enable_session_reinit(true);
+    /// ```
+    pub fn enable_session_reinit(mut self, enable: bool) -> Self {
+        self.enable_session_reinit = enable;
+        self
+    }
 }
 
 impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
@@ -1109,6 +1151,7 @@ impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
             allow_stateless: true,
             auth_header: None,
             custom_headers: HashMap::new(),
+            enable_session_reinit: true,
         }
     }
 }

     /// Custom HTTP headers to include with every request

+    /// If true, the client will transparently re-initialize the session when it
+    /// receives an HTTP 404 (session expired) response. When disabled, a
+    /// [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`] error is propagated instead.
+    ///
+    /// Defaults to `true` to maintain backward compatibility.
+    pub enable_session_reinit: bool,
 }
 
 impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
@@ -1098,6 +1112,34 @@ impl StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
         self.custom_headers = custom_headers;
         self
     }
+
+    /// Enable or disable transparent session re-initialization on HTTP 404.
+    ///
+    /// When enabled, if the server returns a 404 (session expired), the client
+    /// will automatically perform a fresh initialization handshake and replay
+    /// the original request. This is useful for servers that may lose session
+    /// state but can safely re-initialize.
+    ///
+    /// When disabled (the default), a [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`]
+    /// error is propagated to the caller, which can then decide how to handle
+    /// the expired session.
+    ///
+    /// # Arguments
+    ///
+    /// * `enable` - Whether to enable transparent re-initialization
+    ///
+    /// # Example
+    ///
+    /// ```rust,no_run
+    /// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig;
+    ///
+    /// let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp")
+    ///     .enable_session_reinit(true);
+    /// ```
+    pub fn enable_session_reinit(mut self, enable: bool) -> Self {
+        self.enable_session_reinit = enable;
+        self
+    }
 }
 
 impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
@@ -1109,6 +1151,7 @@ impl Default for StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig {
             allow_stateless: true,
             auth_header: None,
             custom_headers: HashMap::new(),
+            enable_session_reinit: true,
         }
     }
 }

+
+    /// Enable or disable transparent session re-initialization on HTTP 404.
+    ///
+    /// When enabled, if the server returns a 404 (session expired), the client
+    /// will automatically perform a fresh initialization handshake and replay
+    /// the original request. This is useful for servers that may lose session
+    /// state but can safely re-initialize.
+    ///
+    /// When disabled (the default), a [`StreamableHttpError::SessionExpired`]
+    /// error is propagated to the caller, which can then decide how to handle
+    /// the expired session.
+    ///
+    /// # Arguments
+    ///
+    /// * `enable` - Whether to enable transparent re-initialization
+    ///
+    /// # Example
+    ///
+    /// ```rust,no_run
+    /// use rmcp::transport::streamable_http_client::StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig;
+    ///
+    /// let config = StreamableHttpClientTransportConfig::with_uri("http://localhost:8000/mcp")
+    ///     .enable_session_reinit(true);
+    /// ```
+    pub fn enable_session_reinit(mut self, enable: bool) -> Self {
+        self.enable_session_reinit = enable;
+        self
+    }
 }
